               </entryFree>26:Tb30,<entryFree id="n44680" key="وَقَّعَ فِى الكِتَابِ" type="main">     
                  <form>       
                     <itype>2</itype>        
                     <orth orig="" extent="full" lang="ar">وَقَّعَ فِى الكِتَابِ</orth>
                     <orth extent="full" lang="ar">ذ</orth>
                  </form>, (MA, TA,) inf. n. <foreign lang="ar">تَوْقِيعٌ</foreign>, (KL, TA,) [as commonly used in the present day,] <hi rend="ital">He signed the writing</hi> [<hi rend="ital">for the purpose of giving effect to it, either beneath, or by endorsing it</hi>]: (MA, KL:) [but as generally used in earlier, though post-classical, times,] <hi rend="ital">he annexed to the writing, after it had been finished, for the</hi> 
                  <pb n="3058"/> 
                  <hi rend="ital">Sultán or the administrator of affairs, to whom it had been submitted, something</hi> [<hi rend="ital">for the purpose of giving effect thereto</hi>]; <hi rend="ital">as, for instance, when a complaint is submitted to the Sultán or to the administrator, and one writes beneath the writing or on the back thereof,</hi> “ <hi rend="ital">Let the affair,</hi> or <hi rend="ital">case, of this person be looked into, and let his right,</hi> or <hi rend="ital">due, be fully exacted for this person:</hi> ” or, accord. to Az, <hi rend="ital">he wrote, upon the writing, a concise abstract, omitting redundances, of the objects of want</hi> [<hi rend="ital">petitioned for therein</hi>]: from <foreign lang="ar">تَوْقِيعُ</foreign> 
                  <foreign lang="ar">الدَّبَرِ ظَهْرَ البَعِيرِ</foreign> [“ the gall's, or sore's, <hi rend="ital">marking</hi> the back of the camel ”]; as though the <foreign lang="ar">مُوَقِّع</foreign> upon the writing marked, upon the case respecting which the writing was written, that which confirmed it, and rendered its execution obligatory: (TA:) <foreign lang="ar">تَوْقِيعٌ</foreign> also signifies such a writing itself (<foreign lang="ar">مَا يُوَقَّعُ فِى كِتَابٍِ</foreign>; S, K, TA;) and its pl. is <foreign lang="ar">تَوْقِيعَاتٌ</foreign>: (TA:) it is said to be an Islámic term; not old Arabic. (TA.) [Also <hi rend="ital">He made an entry of a note</hi> or <hi rend="ital">postil</hi> or <hi rend="ital">the like,</hi> or <hi rend="ital">entries of notes,</hi> &amp;c., <hi rend="ital">in the writing,</hi> or <hi rend="ital">book:</hi> see an ex. voce <foreign lang="ar">ضِعْف</foreign>.          <sense type="b" n="2">-b2-</sense>  <foreign lang="ar">وقّع بِهِ</foreign>
